Trigger("Cats - Revamp by Kupie"){
Conditions:
	Always();

Actions:
	Comment("Maintenance: push unused air units to noair2 zone");
	Move Unit("Current Player", "Magellan (Science Vessel)", All, "noair2", "Start");
	Move Unit("Current Player", "Yggdrasill (Overlord)", All, "noair2", "Start");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("All players"){
Conditions:
	Switch("DifficultyChosen", Set);
	Switch("GameStarted", Not Set);
	Switch("EUDUnitsPlaced", Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Game start: difficulty chosen, begin game");
	Set Countdown Timer(Set To, 80);
	Center View("Start");
	Set Switch("GameStarted", set);
	Set Switch("dt counter", set);
	Set Switch("Rescue", set);
	Set Switch("AntiBS", set);
	Set Switch("Ban", set);
	Set Switch("pylon invuln", set);
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Player 1"){
Conditions:
	Always();

Actions:
	Comment("Init: transfer selection civilian to host (Player 12)");
	Give Units to Player("Player 12", "Current Player", "Terran Civilian", 1, "DifficultyBox");
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Cats - Revamp by Kupie"){
Conditions:
	Command("Player 8", "Protoss Observer", At least, 1);

Actions:
	Comment("AI vision: enable cat player vision scripts");
	Run AI Script("+Vi0");
	Run AI Script("+Vi1");
	Run AI Script("+Vi2");
	Run AI Script("+Vi3");
	Run AI Script("+Vi4");
	Run AI Script("+Vi5");
	Run AI Script("+Vi6");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Cats - Revamp by Kupie"){
Conditions:
	Command("Player 8", "Protoss Observer", Exactly, 0);

Actions:
	Comment("AI vision: disable cat player vision scripts");
	Run AI Script("-Vi0");
	Run AI Script("-Vi1");
	Run AI Script("-Vi2");
	Run AI Script("-Vi3");
	Run AI Script("-Vi4");
	Run AI Script("-Vi5");
	Run AI Script("-Vi6");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006"){
Conditions:
	Always();

Actions:
	Comment("UI: display split mode choice prompt");
	Run AI Script("+Vi7");
	Display Text Message(Always Display, "\x013\x004Spawn 1/7 of normal cats for each player?\r\n\x013\x004<----- Yes | No ----->\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n");
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Player 8"){
Conditions:
	Command("Player 11", "Ragnasaur (Ash World)", At least, 1);

Actions:
	Comment("Ragnasaur: track spawner2 location to unit position");
	Move Location("Player 11", "Ragnasaur (Ash World)", "playground", "spawner2");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006"){
Conditions:
	Switch("GameStarted", Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Game start: spawn player probe");
	Create Unit("Current Player", "Protoss Probe", 1, "Start");
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Player 1"){
Conditions:
	Command("Current Player", "Protoss Probe", Exactly, 0);
	Command("Current Player", "Protoss Shield Battery", Exactly, 0);
	Command("Current Player", "Flag", Exactly, 1);
	Bring("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", "Protoss Probe", "Start", At least, 1);
	Switch("Rescue", Set);
	Switch("Long Invulnerability", Not Set);
	Switch("GameStarted", Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Rescue: save dead player (temp invuln)");
	Kill Unit At Location("Current Player", "Flag", 1, "Start");
	Create Unit("Current Player", "Protoss Probe", 1, "save");
	Center View("Start");
	Display Text Message(Always Display, "\x013\x006- You have been saved -\x006\r\n\x013\x004Temporary Invincibility!\x004\r\n\r\n\x013\x018+20 gas for everyone\x018\r\n");
	Set Resources("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", Add, 20, gas);
	Preserve Trigger();
}

Trigger("Cats - Revamp by Kupie"){
Conditions:
	Countdown Timer(At most, 5);
	Switch("Spawned Kak", Not Set);
	Switch("Switch1", Set);
	Switch("Switch2", Set);
	Switch("Switch3", Set);
	Switch("Switch4", Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Kakaru spawn location 1 selection");
	Create Unit("Player 8", "Kakaru (Twilight)", 1, "1");
	Set Invincibility("Current Player", "Kakaru (Twilight)", "1", enabled);
	Give Units to Player("Current Player", "Player 11", "Kakaru (Twilight)", 1, "1");
	Set Switch("Spawned Kak", set);
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Player 8"){
Conditions:
	Command("Player 11", "Kakaru (Twilight)", At least, 1);

Actions:
	Comment("Kakaru spawn location ? selection");
	Wait(5000);
	Kill Unit("Player 11", "Kakaru (Twilight)");
	Kill Unit("Player 11", "Ragnasaur (Ash World)");
	Set Switch("Spawned Kak", clear);
	Set Switch("Spawned Rag", clear);
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

	Command("Player 11", "Kakaru (Twilight)", At least, 1);

	Move Location("Player 11", "Kakaru (Twilight)", "playground", "spawner");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

Conditions:
	Countdown Timer(At most, 1);
	Switch("GameStarted", Set);

	Comment("Ongoing: persistent state check");
	Set Countdown Timer(Set To, 60);
	Preserve Trigger();
}

Trigger("Player 8"){
Conditions:
	Always();

Actions:
	Comment("Ongoing Switch Randomizer");
	Set Switch("Switch1", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch2", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch3", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch4", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch5", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch6", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch7", randomize);
	Set Switch("Switch8", randomize);
	Set Switch("h1", randomize);

	Bring("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", "Terran Civilian", "ban6", At least, 2);
	Switch("GameStarted", Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Banning Player 6");
	Defeat();
}

Trigger("All players"){
Conditions:
	Always();

Actions:
	Comment("Ongoing: Remove Player 9 units from playground");
	Kill Unit At Location("Player 9", "Protoss Probe", All, "playground");
	Kill Unit At Location("Player 9", "Buildings", All, "playground");
	Kill Unit At Location("Player 9", "Flag", All, "playground");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

	Preserve Trigger();

Trigger("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006"){
Conditions:
	Command("Current Player", "Zerg Lurker Egg", At least, 1);

Actions:
	Comment("Lurker build placer, since we can't just make a lurker direct from a building");
	Move Location("Current Player", "Zerg Lurker Egg", "Anywhere", "Pylon2");
	Remove Unit At Location("Current Player", "Zerg Lurker Egg", 1, "Pylon2");
	Create Unit("Current Player", "Zerg Lurker", 1, "Pylon2");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

//-----------------------------------------------------------------//

Trigger("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006"){
Conditions:
	Command("Current Player", "Zerg Egg", At least, 1);

Actions:
	Comment("Drone build placer for Starports, since we want drones to be expensive from a starport but not from a larva");
	Move Location("Current Player", "Zerg Egg", "Anywhere", "Pylon3");
	Remove Unit At Location("Current Player", "Zerg Egg", 1, "Pylon3");
	Create Unit("Current Player", "Zerg Drone", 1, "Pylon3");
	Preserve Trigger();
}

Trigger("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006"){
Conditions:
	Bring("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", "Terran Civilian", "Easy Mode", At least, 1);
	Switch("SplitModeChoiceMade", Not Set);

Actions:
	Comment("Split mode selection: player chose ENABLED");
	Display Text Message(Always Display, "\x013\x002Split Spawns: ENABLED\r\n\x013\x004Each player triggers 1/7 of normal spawns.");
	Set Switch("ReduceSpawnsForNumPlayers", set);
	Set Switch("SplitModeChoiceMade", set);
	Move Unit("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", "Terran Civilian", 1, "Easy Mode", "DifficultyBox");
	Display Text Message(Always Display, "\r\n\r\n\x013\x004Choose Difficulty!\r\n\x013\x004<----- Easy | Hard ----->\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n\r\n");
}

	Set Resources("Mices - By \x006Hrufnarwa\x006", Add, 50, gas);
	Set Switch("HardModeEnabled", clear);
	Set Switch("EasyModeEnabled", set);
	Set Switch("DifficultyChosen", set);
	Center View("Start");
	Remove Unit At Location("All players", "Any unit", All, "DifficultyBox");
	Center View("Start");
}

	Command("Current Player", "Protoss Shield Battery", Exactly, 0);
	Command("Current Player", "Flag", Exactly, 0);
	Switch("GameStarted", Set);

	Wait(2000);
	Kill Unit At Location("Current Player", "Men", All, "playground");
